 isane na keval upendra kushvaha ko mukhyamantri pad kaa ummidavaar ghoshit karne kii bijepi se apil kii he balki siton ke talmail par bhi apana formula de daalaa, jo bijepi kya kisi bhi rajantik daal ko kabhi manjuur nahin ho saktaa
 In fact, people who know Upendra Kushwaha believe that no one should wonder about the difficulties faced by Kushwaha for BJP, because Kushwaha is not only a very ambitious leader but he is also not happy with not getting the status of Cabinet Minister at the Center
 or jaise-jaise chunaav ke maddenjar bijepi ne endie main or dalon jaise purv mukhyamantri jithan ram maanjhi kii party ko shaamil karaayaa he, usase saafe he ki bijepi ko is baat kaa bharosa he ki lalu-nitish-congress ke saamne wo bina sahyogi dalon ke ek kadam nahin chal sakati or isi kamajori ko bhaanpate hue kushvaha ek ke baad ek har din nai chaal chal rahe hai, jisase unke virodhiyon se zyada bijepi ko safai deni pad rahi he
 On Monday, Rashtriya Janata Dal President Lalu Yadav, who challenges the BJP every day to declare his candidature as Chief Minister, also quipped what was wrong with Kushwaha
 bijepi ke liye pareshaani kii jad main ek or netaa hai ramvilas paswan
 Whether or not Paswan publicly believes it, but not only his ministry but also his former tenure, he believes that this time there is nothing like the past in Paswan nor does Narendra Modi's influence in his ministry
 tippaniyan The second Paswan is unhappy with the arrival of Jeetan Ram Manjhi and that is why he publicly stated that the five mlas of Manjhi who were given ticket in the assembly elections who left his party and joined Janata Dal United , Then he will field his candidates against him
 paswan ne ultimatum maanjhi ko nahin diya he, balki unhone bhartiya janata party ko saafe kar diya he ki tikat ke bantwaare main wo apni manamaani nahin kar sakati
 On the other hand, Manjhi is certainly saddened by the fact that the NDA is being flooded with conditions instead of reception

 But the leaders of Bihar BJP hope that ultimately Prime Minister Narendra Modi will not only take charge of the campaign but will also complete the formalities of convincing the allies and whether the BJP or his ally is currently the last candidate in the competition against Nitish Kumar
 darasal, upendra kushvaha ko jaanane vaale maanate hai ki bijepi ke liye kushvaha kii taraf se mushkilon par kisi ko aashcharya nahin karnaa chahie, kyonki kushvaha na keval ati mahatvakankshi netaa hai balki centre main cabinet mantri kaa darja na milane se wo khush bhi nahin hai
 And as the BJP has inducted more parties such as former Chief Minister Jitan Ram Manjhi's party into the NDA in view of the elections, it is clear that the BJP is confident that it will be in front of lalu-nitish-congress without allies Not taking a step, and realizing this weakness, Kushwaha is going through new moves one after the other, due to which more BJP has to be cleared than his opponents
 somvaar ko rashtriya janata dal adhyaksh lalu yadav, jo har din bijepi ko mukhyamantri kaa apana umidavaar ghoshit karne ke liye chunauti dete hai, unhone bhi chutki lee ki kushvaha main kharabi kya he
 Another leader at the root of the trouble for the BJP is Ram Vilas Paswan
 paswan saarvajanik taur par maane yaa nahin, lekin na keval apane mantralay balki unke purv ke kaarykaal ko dekhne vaale maanate hai ki is baar ke paswan main pehle jaisi koi baat nahin or na hi unke mantralay main narendra modi ke prabhaav ke kaaran chal paati he
 The comments doosraa paswan, jithan ram maanjhi ke aane se bilkul naakhush hai or yahi kaaran he ki unhone saarvajanik rup se kah diya ki maanjhi ke un paanch vidhyaakon ko agar vidhansabha chunaav main tikat diya gaya, jinhone unki party chhodkar janata dal united kaa daaman thama liya tha, tab vah unke khilaaf apane pratyaashee utaarenge
 Paswan has not given the ultimatum to Manjhi, instead he has made it clear to the Bharatiya Janata Party that it cannot do its own arbitrariness in ticket distribution
 vahiin maanjhi is puure ghatnakram se nishchit rup se dukhi hai ki endie main swaagat kii jagah sharton kii bharmaar kii ja rahi he
 In the coming days, if he makes a political drama of getting angry, BJP leaders also believe that no one should wonder about it
